	focus = {
		id = TUR_agricultural_obligation_law
		icon = GFX_focus_SOV_breadbasket_of_the_union
		cost = 5
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_HISTORICAL
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = TUR_transport_anatolian_grain }
		x = 0
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = TUR_transport_anatolian_grain
		available = { any_enemy_country = { is_major = yes } }
		complete_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = TUR_war_agriculture
			unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_abandon_war_agriculture
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_agricultural_obligation_law1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_naval_blockade_reduce_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_agricultural_obligation_law2 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			add_ideas = TUR_war_agriculture
			unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_abandon_war_agriculture
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 2 } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_naval_blockade_reduce_2
					add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.02 }
					add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.01 }
					add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.02 }
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
						add_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
						every_country = {
							limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_dummy }
							remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade_dummy
							add_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade_dummy
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = TUR_agricultural_obligation_law1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade < 3 } }
					remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
					set_country_flag = TUR_agricultural_obligation_law2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { global.TUR_agricultural_obligation_law_naval_blockade = TUR_naval_blockade }
					every_country = {
						limit = { has_idea = TUR_great_famine_of_syria }
						country_event = { id = ottoman.159 hours = 8 }
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade = -2 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}

joint_focus = {
	id = TUR_german_ottoman_military_mission
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_military_mission
	text_icon = joint_GER_TUR_focus_style
	cost = 5
	search_filters = {
		FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_XP
		FOCUS_FILTER_HISTORICAL
	}
	prerequisite = { focus = TUR_continue_german_cooperation focus = GER_finance_berlin_baghdad_railway }
	x = 0
	y = 0
	offset = {
		x = 45
		y = 4
		trigger = { tag = TUR }
	}
	offset = {
		x = -10
		y = 2
		trigger = { original_tag = GER }
	}
	available = {
		TUR = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_our_traditional_allies } }
		GER = {
			is_GER_a_monarchy = yes
			NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }	
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		if = {
			limit = {  original_tag = TUR }
			NOT = { country_exists = GER }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = GER }
			NOT = { country_exists = GER }
		}
	}
	completion_reward_joint_originator = {
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = TUR }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_german_ottoman_military_mission_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_max_command_power_mult = 0.05 }
			GER = { country_event = { id = ww1_liman_affair.1 hours = 8 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = GER }
			army_experience = 25
			country_event = { id = ww1_liman_affair.1 hours = 8 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_send_military_mission_to_ottoman
		effect_tooltip = { GER_TUR_military_mission_effect = yes }
	}
	completion_reward_joint_member = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			army_experience = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TUR }
			TUR = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_german_ottoman_military_mission_tt
				add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_max_command_power_mult = 0.05 }
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 30
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			original_tag = GER
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			original_tag = GER
			date < 1913.1.1
		}
	}
}
